                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref46"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref46" class="rightTabRefNumLink">46</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit46" data-doi="10.1039/C7EE01100H"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Liu, Z. M.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lu, T. C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Song, T.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yu, X. Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lou, X. W.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Paik, U.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Structure-Designed Synthesis of FeS<sub>2</sub>@C Yolk-Shell Nanoboxes as a High-Performance Anode for Sodium-Ion Batteries</span>. <i>Energy Environ. Sci.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2017</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>10</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">1576</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">1580</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/C7EE01100H</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit46R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">46</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Structure-designed synthesis of FeS2@C yolk-shell nanoboxes as a high-performance anode for sodium-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Liu, Zhiming; Lu, Tianchi; Song, Taeseup; Yu, Xin-Yao; Lou, Xiong Wen; Paik, Ungyu</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2017</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">10</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">7</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">1576-1580</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">EESNBY</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1754-5706</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Pyrite (FeS2) is an attractive anode material for sodium-ion batteries (SIBs) with a high theor. capacity of 894 mAh g-1.  However, its practical application is greatly hindered by the rapid capacity fading caused by the large vol. expansion upon sodiation.  Tuning the morphol. and structure at nanoscale and applying a higher cut-off voltage are essential to address this issue.  Here, a facile etching method coupled with a novel sulfidation-in-nanobox strategy is developed to synthesize unique FeS2@C yolk-shell nanoboxes.  The as-obtained FeS2@C nanoboxes reveal excellent sodium storage performance.  The remarkable electrochem. properties are attributed to the elaborate yolk-shell nanoarchitecture.  In particular, it delivers a high specific capacity of 511 mAh g-1 at 100 mA g-1 after 100 cycles.  Furthermore, a high specific capacity of 403 mAh g-1 even at 5 A g-1 is delivered.  Most impressively, a stable capacity of 330 mAh g-1 can still be retained at 2 A g-1 even after 800 cycles.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGrvJjmhFrYQyrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljPH0wBtcprJw"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2sXptFamsL0%253D&amp;md5=36e009c64dd7a8c52d074bf74fb945a8</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref47"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref47" class="rightTabRefNumLink">47</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit47" data-doi="10.1021/acs.chemmater.5b03920"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Hu, L. Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Zhu, X. S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Du, Y. C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Li, Y. F.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Zhou, X. S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Bao, J. C.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">A Chemically Coupled Antimony/Multilayer Graphene Hybrid as a High-Performance Anode for Sodium-Ion Batteries</span>. <i>Chem. Mater.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>27</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">8138</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">8145</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/acs.chemmater.5b03920</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit47R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">47</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">A Chemically Coupled Antimony/Multilayer Graphene Hybrid as a High-Performance Anode for Sodium-Ion Batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Hu, Lingyun; Zhu, Xiaoshu; Du, Yichen; Li, Yafei; Zhou, Xiaosi; Bao, Jianchun</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Chemistry of Materials</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">27</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">23</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">8138-8145</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">CMATEX</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0897-4756</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Chemical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Na-ion batteries have recently attracted considerable attention as a promising alternative to Li-ion batteries owing to the natural abundance and low cost of Na compared with Li.  Among all proposed anode materials for Na-ion batteries, Sb is a desirable candidate due to its high theor. capacity (660 mA h g-1).  Herein, an Sb/multilayer graphene hybrid, in which Sb is homogeneously anchored on multilayer graphene, is produced by a confined vapor deposition method.  The chem. bonding can realize robust and intimate contact between Sb and multilayer graphene, and the uniform distribution of Sb and the highly conductive and flexible multilayer graphene can not only improve Na ion diffusion and electronic transport but also stabilize the solid electrolyte interphase upon the large vol. changes of Sb during cycling.  Consequently, the Sb/multilayer graphene hybrid shows a high reversible Na storage capacity (452 mA h g-1 at a c.d. of 100 mA g-1), stable long-term cycling performance with 90% capacity retention after 200 cycles, and excellent rate capability (210 mA h g-1 under 5000 mA g-1).  This facile synthesis approach and unique nanostructure can potentially be extended to other alloy materials for Na-ion batteries.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqDfBd8kZiyFbVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljPH0wBtcprJw"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXhvVCjtb7K&amp;md5=2d783871704dc4fcc47474721f1b1ab3</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref48"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref48" class="rightTabRefNumLink">48</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit48" data-doi="10.1039/C3EE44004D"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">You, Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Wu, X. L.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yin, Y. X.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Guo, Y. G.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">High-Quality Prussian Blue Crystals as Superior Cathode Materials for Room-Temperature Sodium-Ion Batteries</span>. <i>Energy Environ. Sci.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2014</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>7</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">1643</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">1647</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/C3EE44004D</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit48R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">48</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">High-quality Prussian blue crystals as superior cathode materials for room-temperature sodium-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">You, Ya; Wu, Xing-Long; Yin, Ya-Xia; Guo, Yu-Guo</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Energy &amp; Environmental Science</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2014</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">7</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">5</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">1643-1647</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">EESNBY</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1754-5706</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">High-quality Prussian blue crystals with a small no. of vacancies and a low water content are obtained by employing Na4Fe(CN)6 as the single iron-source precursor.  The high-quality Prussian blue shows high specific capacity and remarkable cycling stability as the cathode material for Na-ion batteries because of its excellent ion storage capability and impressive structure stability.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGrwChCr1X936rVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljPH0wBtcprJw"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2cXmslyqtr4%253D&amp;md5=8ef56fe4bdaddf3b82601f7407c402b3</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref49"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref49" class="rightTabRefNumLink">49</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit49" data-doi="10.1002/adfm.201600747"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Jiang, Y. Z.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yu, S. L.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Wang, B. Q.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Li, Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Sun, W. P.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lu, Y. H.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yan, M.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Song, B.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Dou, S. X.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Prussian Blue@C Composite as an Ultrahigh-Rate and Long-Life Sodium-Ion Battery Cathode</span>. <i>Adv. Funct. Mater.</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>26</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">5315</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">5321</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1002/adfm.201600747</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit49R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">49</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Prussian Blue@C Composite as an Ultrahigh-Rate and Long-Life Sodium-Ion Battery Cathode</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Jiang, Yinzhu; Yu, Shenglan; Wang, Baoqi; Li, Yong; Sun, Wenping; Lu, Yunhao; Yan, Mi; Song, Bin; Dou, Shixue</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Advanced Functional Materials</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2016</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">26</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">29</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">5315-5321</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">AFMDC6</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1616-301X</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Wiley-VCH Verlag GmbH &amp; Co. KGaA</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Rechargeable sodium ion batteries (SIBs) are surfacing as promising candidates for applications in large-scale energy-storage systems.  Prussian blue (PB) and its analogs (PBAs) have been considered as potential cathodes because of their rigid open framework and low-cost synthesis.  Nevertheless, PBAs suffer from inferior rate capability and poor cycling stability resulting from the low electronic cond. and deficiencies in the PBAs framework.  Herein, to understand the vacancy-impacted sodium storage and Na-insertion reaction kinetics, we report on an in-situ synthesized PB@C composite as a high-performance SIB cathode.  Perfectly shaped, nanosized PB cubes were grown directly on carbon chains, assuring fast charge transfer and Na-ion diffusion.  The existence of [Fe(CN)6] vacancies in the PB crystal is found to greatly degrade the electrochem. activity of the FeLS(C) redox couple via first-principles computation.  Superior reaction kinetics are demonstrated for the redox reactions of the FeHS(N) couple, which rely on the partial insertion of Na ions to enhance the electron conduction.  The synergistic effects of the structure and morphol. results in the PB@C composite achieving an unprecedented rate capability and outstanding cycling stability (77.5 mAh g-1 at 90 C, 90 mAh g-1 after 2000 cycles at 20 C with 90% capacity retention).</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGo693UCkOhO2rVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0ljPH0wBtcprJw"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC28Xot1Khtbo%253D&amp;md5=f90bf6c154f4b4dbd6247e7e07f0de7c</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref50"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref50" class="rightTabRefNumLink">50</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit50" data-doi="10.1039/c3ta12036h"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Wu, X. Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Deng, W. W.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Qian, J. F.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Cao, Y. L.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Ai, X. P.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yang, H. X.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Single-Crystal FeFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> Nanoparticles: A High Capacity and High Rate Cathode for Na-Ion Batteries</span>. <i>J. Mater. Chem. A</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2013</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>1</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">10130</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">10134</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1039/c3ta12036h</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit50R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">50</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Single-crystal FeFe(CN)6 nanoparticles: a high capacity and high rate cathode for Na-ion batteries</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Wu, Xianyong; Deng, Wenwen; Qian, Jiangfeng; Cao, Yuliang; Ai, Xinping; Yang, Hanxi</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Materials Chemistry A: Materials for Energy and Sustainability</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2013</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">1</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">35</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">10130-10134</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JMCAET</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">2050-7496</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Royal Society of Chemistry</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Prussian blue analogs are actively explored as low cost and high capacity cathodes for Na ion batteries; however, their applications are hindered by low capacity use and poor cyclability of these compds.  This problem can be solved by controlling the purity and crystallinity of the Prussian blue lattices.  As a model compd., single-crystal FeIIIFeIII(CN)6 nanoparticles are synthesized and found to have a sufficiently high capacity of 120 mA-h g-1, an exceptional rate capability at 20 C and superior cyclability with 87% capacity retention over 500 cycles, showing great promise for Na ion battery applications.  More significantly, these results provide a new insight into the intercalation chem. of Prussian blue analogs and open new perspectives to develop Na storage cathodes for widespread applications of elec. energy storage.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGqcqkhMgh8BhrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lhh0vIHwx_FBQ"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC3sXht1OqsLfL&amp;md5=46ba31a8957255cb823e0bb80a812a45</span></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i14">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge on the <a href="/" class="ext-link">ACS Publications website</a> at DOI: <a href="/doi/abs/10.1021/acsnano.8b03541" class="ext-link">10.1021/acsnano.8b03541</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Morphology and phase characterization of NiS<sub>1.03</sub> PHCs and FeFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>;         <script nonce="90f6ee782dc0775c-SJC">
(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

</script>

// LIT-455776 workaround
// Moving the popup before the header content for tab accessibility
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    const headerNode = $('.header_content');
    const popupNode = $('.pairing-affiliations-popup');

    if (!headerNode.length || !popupNode.length)
        return;

        <!-- <h2>System Message</h2> -->
        <span class="system-message-date">Sunday, February 09, 2025</span>
        <p>Please be aware that pubs.acs.org is undergoing maintenance from Saturday February 1 to Monday Febraury 3, that may have an impact on your experience. During this time, you may not be able to access certain features like login, purchasing single articles, saving searches or running existing saved searches, modifying your e-Alert preferences, or accessing Librarian administrative functions. <script nonce="90f6ee782dc0775c-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90f6ee782dc0775c-SJC">
"use strict"
//Script checks gdpr cookie and submits form
	/* 
	Create an in-page pop-up message, only for the InfoCentral homepage, that will gather email registrants for the library marketing list.
	 
	Needs the end point
	*/

var infoCentralCapture = (function() {

    //Detect mobile device
    window.mobilecheck = function() {
        var check = false;
        (function(a){if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|iris|kindle|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|mobile.+firefox|netfront|opera )|avan|be(ck|ll|nq)|bi(lb|rd)|bl(ac|az)|br(e|v)w|bumb|bw\-(n|u)|c55\/|capi|ccwa|cdm\-|cell|chtm|cldc|cmd\-|co(mp|nd)|craw|da(it|ll|ng)|dbte|dc\-s|devi|dica|dmob|do(c|p)o|ds(12|\-d)|el(49|ai)|em(l2|ul)|er(ic|k0)|esl8|ez([4-7]0|os|wa|ze)|fetc|fly(\-|_)|g1 u|g560|gene|gf\-5|g\-mo|go(\.w|od)|gr(ad|un)|haie|hcit|hd\-(m|p|t)|hei\-|hi(pt|ta)|hp( i|ip)|hs\-c|ht(c(\-| |_|a|g|p|s|t)|tp)|hu(aw|tc)|i\-(20|go|ma)|i230|iac( |\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90f6ee782dc0775c-SJC">
var currentJournal = "ACS Nano";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>

$(document).ready(function(){
    var cookie = "";
    var uri = "/doi/full/10.1021/html_original_uri?id=123";
    console.log("ACSPubs2 start");
    $.getJSON('https://extreme-ip-lookup.com/json/', function(data, status) {
            if ( status == 'success' ) {
                $.each(data, function(i, field){
                    cookie=cookie.concat(i+' = '+field+" - ");
                });
                
            } else {
                    cookie=status;
            }

            cookie1 = cookie;
            cookie = cookie1 + "; path=/; domain=.acs.org";
            //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
            $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
            //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
            console.log("ACSPubs2 success");
    })
    .fail(function(xx, status, err){
        cookie="error: 127.0.0.1";
        //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
        $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
        console.log("ACSPubs2 failed");
        //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
    });
});    
</script>
